Practicing slow deep breathing exercises can help with anxiety it has helped me tremendously, consistency is key. Everyday set out 15-30 minutes to just breathe. No woo woo esoteric breathing just normal deep breathes without any mental exercises, just breathe in and hold for 8-10 seconds and then exhale very slowly, slower is better, more of the parasympathetic nervous system is activated causing you to relax. Repeat for 15-30 minutes. Patience and discipline is required. CAUTION I do not recommend any fast paced breathing exercises like Whim Hoff's method, those can cause altered states and cause your nervous system to become excited instead of relaxed.

This interview made me uncomfortable, because it felt too scripted or something. Severe anxiety is crippling, disabling, and makes you feel like you're dying. You get dizzy, vertigo, lose all sense of up and down and become spatially disoriented, your heart pounds and palpitate and you gasped desperately for air as the flood of tsunami-like waves crash over you, crushing you, you can experience numbness, and you feel like you are going to faint (and might!) Noise and activity around you becomes extremely over stimulating, and it becomes unbearable. Loud noises, crowds, too many people, too much activity becomes intolerable. Full blown panic sets in. I know this feeling all too well. I also have Babesia, Lyme Disease and other tick borne infections, and one of the classic symptoms of Babesia is air hunger and debilitating anxiety. I mention this, as there can be a missed underlying cause. The best tip I've had for social anxiety are exercises that take you out of your head and into the present physical moment, like noting 5 things in the room that you can see, hear, touch, smell and taste.
